  `breeder_id` int(10) NOT NULL,

CREATE TABLE `breeder_ship_preferences` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `breeder_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',

  KEY `idx_breeder_ship_pref_breeder_id` (`breeder_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1373 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci COMMENT='Join table for the breeders selections of their ship preferences'

CREATE TABLE `breed_ratings` (
  `breed` smallint(6) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Grooming Requirements` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Energy` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Friendliness` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Training Aptitude` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Affection` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Ease of Training` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Intelligence` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Shedding` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Watchdog Ability` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Guard Dog Ability` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Popularity` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Size` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Agility` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Friendly with Kids` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Exercise Requirements` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Friendly with Dogs` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Friendly with Other Pets` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Cold Tolerance` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Heat Tolerance` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`breed`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `content` (
  `id` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `date` date NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00',
  `site` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `url` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `headline` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `byline` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `story` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `type` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `subdomain` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `breed` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `state` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `meta_title` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `meta_keywords` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `meta_description` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `edited_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `date` (`date`),
  KEY `breed_type` (`breed`,`type`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=4975 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci




======elapsed time for MysqlQuery: 0.05 seconds 

*******StartQuery
 drop table if exists buypuppy_puppies."content";
CREATE TABLE buypuppy_puppies."content" (
  "id" int   NOT NULL ,
  "date" date NOT NULL ,
  "site" varchar(255) ,
  "url" varchar(255) ,
  "headline" varchar(255) ,
  "byline" varchar(255) ,
  "story" text ,
  "type" varchar(50) ,
  "subdomain" varchar(50) ,
  "breed" varchar(50) ,
  "state" varchar(50) ,
  "meta_title" varchar(255) ,
  "meta_keywords" text ,
  "meta_description" text ,
  "edited_at" timestamp NULL ,
  PRIMARY KEY ("id")
)

  `sent_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `contact_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `email_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `schedule_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `tracker_ip` varchar(15) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `tracker_hash` char(40) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `tracker_action` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  `tracker_image` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `tracker_user_agent` tinytext COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci,
  `tracker_host` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `tracker_request_uri` tinytext COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci,
  `tracker_timestamp` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`tracker_id`),
  KEY `sent_id` (`sent_id`),
  KEY `contact_id` (`contact_id`),
  KEY `tracker_hash` (`tracker_hash`),
  KEY `tracker_ip` (`tracker_ip`),
  KEY `schedule_id` (`schedule_id`),
  KEY `email_id` (`email_id`),
  KEY `tracker_action` (`tracker_action`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2687321 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `pm_history` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'ID',
  `table` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Event''s table',
  `row_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Event''s row',
  `type` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Type of event',
  `user` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Who did it',
  `field` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Table field if applicable',
  `old` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'Old value if applicable',
  `new` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'New value or description',
  `when` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00' COMMENT 'Event date and time',
  `approved` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `user` (`user`),
  KEY `field` (`field`),

CREATE TABLE `history` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'ID',
  `table` varchar(61) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `row_id` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Event''s row',
  `type` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Type of event',
  `user` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Who did it',
  `field` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Table field if applicable',
  `old` longtext COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci COMMENT 'Old value if applicable',
  `new` longtext COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci COMMENT 'New value or description',
  `when` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Event date and time',
  `hidden` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `ip` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `row_id2` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `type` (`type`),
  KEY `user` (`user`),
  KEY `field` (`field`),
  KEY `ip` (`ip`),
  KEY `row_table_type_field` (`row_id`,`table`,`type`,`field`),
  KEY `when_table_row_type_field` (`when`,`table`,`row_id`,`type`,`field`),
  KEY `when_user_type_table` (`when`,`user`,`type`,`table`),
  KEY `when_type_field_table` (`when`,`type`,`field`,`table`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=39528842 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `lookup` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Auto-inc. ID',
  `user` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'User ID',
  `table` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'DB table',
  `page` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Which HTML form',
  `index` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Field order in the HTML form',
  `field` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `operator` varchar(10) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '=',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `user_table_page_index` (`user`,`table`,`page`,`index`),
  KEY `table` (`table`),
  KEY `page` (`page`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1960395 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

  KEY `contact_timestamp` (`contact_id`,`sent_timestamp`),
  KEY `status_schedule` (`sent_status`,`schedule_id`),
  KEY `timestamp_schedule_status` (`sent_timestamp`,`schedule_id`,`sent_status`),
  KEY `schedule_timestamp_status` (`schedule_id`,`sent_timestamp`,`sent_status`),
  KEY `schedule_status` (`schedule_id`,`sent_status`),
  KEY `timestamp_status` (`sent_timestamp`,`sent_status`),
  KEY `actions_processed` (`actions_processed`)

CREATE TABLE `email` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `template` varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `from` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '"{SESSION_FIRSTNAME}" <{SESSION_EMAIL}>',
  `to` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '"{FIRST_NAME} {LAST_NAME}" <{EMAIL_LOGIN}>',
  `cc` varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `bcc` varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `subject` varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `message` longtext COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `attachment` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `responsive` tinyint(1) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `is_customizable` tinyint(1) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `server` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `type1` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Admin permissions',
  `type2` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Office permissions',
  `type3` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Breeder permissions',
  `type4` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Sales permissions',
  `type5` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `type6` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Breeders/Sales',
  `type7` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'reception',
  `folder` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'contact',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `template` (`template`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=486 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `field` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `table` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Field''s DB table',
  `name` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Field''s DB name',
  `table_id_column` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'id',
  `display` varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Field''s user-friendly name',
  `inputtype` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Type of HTML form input to use',
  `is_nullable` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `is_unique` tinyint(1) unsigned DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Truthy if referenced column has unique constraint',
  `default` varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `attributes` varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Form input''s HTML attributes',
  `startyear` varchar(4) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'For dates only',
  `encoding` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'e.g., urlencode',
  `order` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Field''s order in HTML form',
  `page` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Which HTML form the field is in',
  `type1` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT 'Admin',
  `type2` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Office',
  `type3` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Breeder Accounts',
  `type4` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Sales',

CREATE TABLE `history` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'ID',
  `table` varchar(61) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `row_id` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Event''s row',
  `type` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Type of event',
  `user` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Who did it',
  `field` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Table field if applicable',
  `old` longtext COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci COMMENT 'Old value if applicable',
  `new` longtext COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci COMMENT 'New value or description',
  `when` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Event date and time',
  `hidden` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `ip` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `row_id2` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `type` (`type`),
  KEY `user` (`user`),
  KEY `field` (`field`),
  KEY `ip` (`ip`),
  KEY `row_table_type_field` (`row_id`,`table`,`type`,`field`),
  KEY `when_table_row_type_field` (`when`,`table`,`row_id`,`type`,`field`),
  KEY `when_user_type_table` (`when`,`user`,`type`,`table`),
  KEY `when_type_field_table` (`when`,`type`,`field`,`table`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=39528943 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `pm_history` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'ID',
  `table` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Event''s table',
  `row_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Event''s row',
  `type` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Type of event',
  `user` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Who did it',
  `field` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'Table field if applicable',
  `old` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'Old value if applicable',
  `new` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'New value or description',
  `when` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00' COMMENT 'Event date and time',
  `approved` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `user` (`user`),
  KEY `field` (`field`),
  KEY `approved` (`approved`),
  KEY `type` (`type`),
  KEY `row_table_type_field` (`row_id`,`table`,`type`,`field`),
  KEY `when_table_row_type_field` (`when`,`table`,`row_id`,`type`,`field`),
  KEY `when_user_type_table` (`when`,`user`,`type`,`table`),
  KEY `when_type_field_table` (`when`,`type`,`field`,`table`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=35748146 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

  `contact_id` int(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `to_phone` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,

  `message` varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `inbound` tinyint(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  `outbound` tinyint(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  `viewed` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `date` (`date`),
  KEY `outbound` (`outbound`),
  KEY `inbound` (`inbound`),
  KEY `from_phone` (`from_phone`),
  KEY `to_phone` (`to_phone`),
  KEY `contact_id` (`contact_id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `user_viewed_inbound` (`user_id`,`viewed`,`inbound`),
  KEY `folder` (`folder`),
  KEY `sid` (`sid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=726495 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `travels` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `contact_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `puppy_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `preferred_travel_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `breeder_plans_to_ship_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `reply_received` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `updated_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_travel` (`contact_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `_fk_travel_ref_contact` FOREIGN KEY (`contact_id`) REFERENCES `contact` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `travel_airport_prefs` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `travel_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `airport_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `pref_order` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `updated_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_travel_airport_pref` (`travel_id`),
  KEY `idx_travel_airport_pref_0` (`airport_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_travel_airport_prefs_ref_airports` FOREIGN KEY (`airport_id`) REFERENCES `airports` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_travel_airport_prefs_ref_travels` FOREIGN KEY (`travel_id`) REFERENCES `travels` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

Affected rows (SELECT): 1
CREATE TABLE `travel_flights` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `departure_airport_id` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `arrival_airport_id` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `airline_id` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `flight_num` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `flight_air_waybill` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `flight_confirmation` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `departure_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `arrival_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `updated_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_travel_flights_1` (`departure_airport_id`),
  KEY `idx_travel_flights_0` (`arrival_airport_id`),
  KEY `idx_travel_flights` (`airline_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_travel_flights_ref_airlines` FOREIGN KEY (`airline_id`) REFERENCES `airlines` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_travel_flights_ref_airports` FOREIGN KEY (`departure_airport_id`) REFERENCES `airports` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_travel_flights_ref_airports_arrival` FOREIGN KEY (`arrival_airport_id`) REFERENCES `airports` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `user_event` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `field` enum('active','pfinder_active','prequest_active','phoneless_active','email_active','contact_active','west_active','after_hours_active') COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
  `value` enum('yes','no') COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'yes',
  `when` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `recurring` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `active` enum('yes','no') COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'yes',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `when` (`when`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=4791 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci

CREATE TABLE `videos` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `classified_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `wistia_id` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `thumbnail_url` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `thumbnail_width` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `thumbnail_height` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `approved` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `rejected` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `expired` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `notes` varchar(500) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_uploaded` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `approved_expired_puppy_id` (`approved`,`expired`,`classified_id`,`id`),
  KEY `puppy` (`classified_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=42395 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci
